Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-112(5)(b)(i): the objective of the term is unconscionable or against public policy; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-112(5)(b)(ii): the means to achieve the term's objective is unconscionable or against public policy.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-113 Operating agreement -- Effect on limited liability company and person becoming member -- Preformation agreement.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-113(1): A limited liability company is bound by and may enforce the operating agreement, whether or not the limited liability company has itself manifested assent to the operating agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-113(2): A person that becomes a member of a limited liability company is deemed to assent to the operating agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-113(3): Two or more persons intending to become the initial members of a limited liability company may make an agreement providing that upon the formation of the limited liability company the agreement will become the operating agreement.  One person intending to become the initial member of a limited liability company may assent to terms providing that upon the formation of the limited liability company the terms will become the operating agreement.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114 Operating agreement -- Effect on third parties and relationship to records effective on behalf of limited liability company.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114(1): An operating agreement may specify that its amendment requires the approval of a person that is not a party to the operating agreement or the satisfaction of a condition.  An amendment is ineffective if its adoption does not include the required approval or satisfy the specified condition.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114(2): 48-3a-503(2)(b) The obligations of a limited liability company and its members to a person in the person's capacity as a transferee or a person dissociated as a member are governed by the operating agreement.  Subject only to a court order issued under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114(2)(a): is effective with regard to any debt, obligation, or other liability of the limited liability company or its members to the person in the person's capacity as a transferee or person dissociated as a member; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114(2)(b): is not effective to the extent the amendment imposes a new debt, obligation, or other liability on the transferee or person dissociated as a member.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114(3): 48-3a-112(3); (4)(c) If a record delivered by a limited liability company to the division for filing becomes effective and contains a provision that would be ineffective under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114(4): (3) Subject to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114(4)(a): the operating agreement prevails as to members, persons dissociated as members, transferees, and managers; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-114(4)(b): the record prevails as to other persons to the extent they reasonably rely on the record.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-115 Delivery of record.
---------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-115(1): Except as otherwise provided in this chapter, permissible means of delivery of a record include delivery by hand, the United States Postal Service, a commercial delivery service, and electronic transmission.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-115(2): Delivery to the division is effective only when a record is received by the division.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-116 Reservation of power to amend or repeal.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
The Legislature of this state has power to amend or repeal all or part of this chapter at any time, and all domestic and foreign limited liability companies subject to this chapter are governed by the amendment or repeal.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-201 Formation of limited liability company -- Certificate of organization.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-201(4): A limited liability company is formed when the limited liability company's certificate of organization becomes effective and at least one person becomes a member.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205 Filing requirements.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(1): To be filed by the division pursuant to this chapter, a record must be received by the division, comply with this chapter, and satisfy the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(1)(a): The filing of the record must be required or permitted by this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(1)(b): The record must be physically delivered in written form unless and to the extent the division permits electronic delivery of records.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(1)(c): The record must be typewritten or computer generated.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(1)(d): The words in the record must be in English, and numbers must be in Arabic or Roman numerals, but the name of an entity need not be in English if written in English letters or Arabic or Roman numerals.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(1)(e): The record must be signed by a person authorized or required under this chapter to sign the record.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(1)(f): The record must state the name and capacity, if any, of each individual who signed it, either on behalf of the individual or the person authorized or required to sign the record, but need not contain a seal, attestation, acknowledgment, or verification.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(2): If law other than this chapter prohibits the disclosure by the division of information contained in a record delivered to the division for filing, the division shall accept the record if the record otherwise complies with this chapter, but the division may redact the information.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(3): When a record is delivered to the division for filing, any fee required under this chapter and any fee, tax, interest, or penalty required to be paid under this chapter or law other than this chapter must be paid in a manner permitted by the division or by that law.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-205(4): The division may require that a record delivered in written form be accompanied by an identical or conformed copy.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-206 Effective time and date.
--------------------------------------------------------
Except as otherwise provided in SectionUtah Code Annotated § 48-3a-206(1): 48-3a-209 on the date and at the time of its filing by the division, as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-206(2): (1) on the date of filing and at the time specified in the record as its effective time, if later than the time under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-206(3): at a specified delayed effective date and time, which may not be more than 90 days after the date of filing; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-206(4): if a delayed effective date is specified, but no time is specified, at 12:01 a.m. on the date specified, which may not be more than 90 days after the date of filing.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-207 Withdrawal of filed record before effectiveness.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-207(2)(c): if signed by fewer than all the persons that signed the record being withdrawn, state that the record is withdrawn in accordance with the agreement of all the persons that signed the record.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-207(3): On filing by the division of a statement of withdrawal, the action or transaction evidenced by the original record does not take effect.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208 Correcting filed record.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(1): A person on whose behalf a filed record was delivered to the division for filing may correct the record if:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(1)(a): the record at the time of filing was inaccurate;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(1)(b): the record was defectively signed; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(1)(c): the electronic transmission of the record to the division was defective.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(2): To correct a filed record, a person on whose behalf the record was delivered to the division must deliver to the division for filing a statement of correction.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(3): A statement of correction:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(3)(a): may not state a delayed effective date;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(3)(b): must be signed by the person correcting the filed record;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(3)(c): must identify the filed record to be corrected;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(3)(d): must specify the inaccuracy or defect to be corrected; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(3)(e): must correct the inaccuracy or defect.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-208(4): 48-3a-103(4) A statement of correction is effective as of the effective date of the filed record that it corrects except for purposes of Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209 Duty of division to file -- Review of refusal to file -- Transmission of information by division.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(1): The division shall file a record delivered to the division for filing which satisfies this chapter.  The duty of the division under this section is ministerial.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(2): When the division files a record, the division shall record it as filed on the date and at the time of its delivery.  After filing a record, the division shall deliver to the person that submitted the record a copy of the record with an acknowledgment of the date and time of filing and, in the case of a statement of denial, also to the limited liability company to which the statement pertains.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(3): If the division refuses to file a record, the division shall, not later than 15 business days after the record is delivered:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(3)(a): return the record or notify the person that submitted the record of the refusal; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(3)(b): provide a brief explanation in a record of the reason for the refusal.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(4): Title 78A, Judiciary and Judicial Administration
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(4)(a): Title 78A, Judiciary and Judicial Administration If the division refuses to file a record, the person that submitted the record may petition a court with jurisdiction under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(4)(b): The record and the explanation of the division of the refusal to file must be attached to the petition.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(4)(c): The court may decide the matter in a summary proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(5): The filing of or refusal to file a record does not create a presumption that the information contained in the record is correct or incorrect.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(6): 16-17-301 Except as otherwise provided by Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(6)(a): in person to the person that submitted it;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(6)(b): to the address of the person's registered agent;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(6)(c): to the principal office of the person; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-209(6)(d): to another address the person provides to the division for delivery.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-212(5): 16-17-206 If an annual report contains the name or address of a registered agent which differs from the information shown in the records of the division immediately before the annual report becomes effective, the differing information in the annual report is considered a statement of change under Section


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-301 No agency powers of member as member.
---------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-301(1): A member is not an agent of a limited liability company solely by reason of being a member.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-301(2): A person's status as a member does not prevent or restrict law other than this chapter from imposing liability on a limited liability company because of the person's conduct.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302 Statement of authority.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(1): A limited liability company may deliver to the division for filing a statement of authority.  The statement:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(1)(a): must include the name of the limited liability company and the street and mailing addresses of its registered agent;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(1)(b): with respect to any position that exists in or with respect to the limited liability company, may state the authority, or limitations on the authority, of all persons holding the position to:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(1)(b)(i): execute an instrument transferring real property held in the name of the limited liability company; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(1)(b)(ii): enter into other transactions on behalf of, or otherwise act for or bind, the limited liability company; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(1)(c): may state the authority, or limitations on the authority, of a specific person to:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(1)(c)(i): execute an instrument transferring real property held in the name of the limited liability company; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(1)(c)(ii): enter into other transactions on behalf of, or otherwise act for or bind, the limited liability company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(2): To amend or cancel a statement of authority filed by the division, a limited liability company must deliver to the division for filing an amendment or cancellation stating:

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(2)(c): the date the statement being affected became effective; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(2)(d): the contents of the amendment or a declaration that the statement is canceled.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-302(3): A statement of authority affects only the power of a person to bind a limited liability company to persons that are not members.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-303 Statement of denial.
----------------------------------------------------
A person named in a filed statement of authority granting that person authority may deliver to the division for filing a statement of denial that:Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-303(1): provides the name of the limited liability company and the caption of the statement of authority to which the statement of denial pertains; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-303(2): denies the grant of authority.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-304 Liability of members and managers.
------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-304(1): (1) A debt, obligation, or other liability of a limited liability company is solely the debt, obligation, or other liability of the limited liability company.  A member or manager is not personally liable, directly or indirectly, by way of contribution or otherwise, for a debt, obligation, or other liability of the limited liability company solely by reason of being or acting as a member or manager.  This Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-304(2): The failure of a limited liability company to observe formalities relating to the exercise of its powers or management of its activities and affairs is not a ground for imposing liability on a member or manager of the limited liability company for a debt, obligation, or other liability of the limited liability company.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401 Becoming a member.
--------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(1): If a limited liability company is to have only one member upon formation, the person becomes a member as agreed by that person and the organizer of the limited liability company.  That person and the organizer may be, but need not be, different persons.  If different, the organizer acts on behalf of the initial member.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(2): If a limited liability company is to have more than one member upon formation, those persons become members as agreed by the persons before the formation of the limited liability company.  The organizer acts on behalf of the persons in forming the limited liability company and may be, but need not be, one of the persons.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(3): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication; 48-3a-701(3) After formation of a limited liability company, a person becomes a member:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(3)(a): as provided in the operating agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(3)(b): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication as the result of a transaction effective under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(3)(c): with the consent of all the members; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(3)(d): 48-3a-701(3) as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(4): A person may become a member without:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(4)(a): acquiring a transferable interest; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-401(4)(b): making or being obligated to make a contribution to the limited liability company.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-402 Form of contribution.
-----------------------------------------------------
A contribution may consist of property transferred to, services performed for, or another benefit provided to the limited liability company or an agreement to transfer property to, perform services for, or provide another benefit to the company.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-403 Liability for contributions.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-403(1): A person's obligation to make a contribution to a limited liability company is not excused by the person's death, disability, or other inability to perform personally.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-403(2): If a person does not fulfill an obligation to make a contribution other than money, the person is obligated at the option of the limited liability company to contribute money equal to the value of the part of the contribution which has not been made.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-403(3): (1); (3) The obligation of a person to make a contribution may be compromised only by consent of all members.  If a creditor of a limited liability company extends credit or otherwise acts in reliance on an obligation described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-404 Sharing of and right to distributions before dissolution.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-404(1): 48-3a-502; 48-3a-503 Any distributions made by a limited liability company before its dissolution and winding up must be in equal shares among members and persons dissociated as members, except to the extent necessary to comply with a transfer effective under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-404(2): A person has a right to a distribution before the dissolution and winding up of a limited liability company only if the limited liability company decides to make an interim distribution.  A person's dissociation does not entitle the person to a distribution.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-404(3): 48-3a-711(4) A person does not have a right to demand or receive a distribution from a limited liability company in any form other than money.  Except as otherwise provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-404(4): If a member or transferee becomes entitled to receive a distribution, the member or transferee has the status of, and is entitled to all remedies available to, a creditor of the limited liability company with respect to the distribution.  However, the limited liability company's obligation to make a distribution is subject to offset for any amount owed to the limited liability company by the member or a person dissociated as a member on whose account the distribution is made.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-405 Limitation on distributions.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-405(1): 48-3a-711 A limited liability company may not make a distribution, including a distribution under Section

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407 Management of limited liability company.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(1): A limited liability company is a member-managed limited liability company unless the operating agreement:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(1)(a): expressly provides that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(1)(a)(i): the limited liability company is or will be "manager-managed";
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(1)(a)(ii): the limited liability company is or will be "managed by managers"; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(1)(a)(iii): management of the limited liability company is or will be "vested in managers"; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(1)(b): includes words of similar import.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(2): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication In a member-managed limited liability company, the following rules apply:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(2)(a): Except as otherwise provided in this chapter, the management and conduct of the limited liability company are vested in the members.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(2)(b): Each member has equal rights in the management and conduct of the limited liability company's activities and affairs.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(2)(c): A difference arising among members as to a matter in the ordinary course of the activities of the limited liability company shall be decided by a majority of the members.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(2)(d): An act outside the ordinary course of the activities and affairs of the limited liability company may be undertaken only with the affirmative vote or consent of all members.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(2)(e): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication The affirmative vote or consent of all members is required to approve a transaction under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(2)(f): The operating agreement may be amended only with the affirmative vote or consent of all members.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication In a manager-managed limited liability company, the following rules apply:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(a): Except as expressly provided in this chapter, any matter relating to the activities and affairs of the limited liability company is decided exclusively by the manager, or, if there is more than one manager, by a majority of the managers.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(b): Each manager has equal rights in the management and conduct of the limited liability company's activities and affairs.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(c): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication The affirmative vote or consent of all members is required to:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(c)(i): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication approve a transaction under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(c)(ii): undertake any act outside the ordinary course of the limited liability company's activities and affairs; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(c)(iii): amend the operating agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(d): A manager may be chosen at any time by the consent of a majority of the members and remains a manager until a successor has been chosen, unless the manager at an earlier time resigns, is removed, or dies, or, in the case of a manager that is not an individual, terminates.  A manager may be removed at any time by the consent of a majority of the members without notice or cause.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(e): A person need not be a member to be a manager, but the dissociation of a member that is also a manager removes the person as a manager.  If a person that is both a manager and a member ceases to be a manager, that cessation does not by itself dissociate the person as a member.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(3)(f): A person's ceasing to be a manager does not discharge any debt, obligation, or other liability to the limited liability company or members which the person incurred while a manager.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(4): An action requiring the vote or consent of members under this chapter may be taken without a meeting, and a member may appoint a proxy or other agent to vote, consent, or otherwise act for the member by signing an appointing record, personally or by the member's agent.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(5): The dissolution of a limited liability company does not affect the applicability of this section.  However, a person that wrongfully causes dissolution of the limited liability company loses the right to participate in management as a member and a manager.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(6): A limited liability company shall reimburse a member for an advance to the limited liability company beyond the amount of capital the member agreed to contribute.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(7): (6); 48-3a-408(1) A payment or advance made by a member which gives rise to an obligation of the limited liability company under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-407(8): A member is not entitled to remuneration for services performed for a member-managed limited liability company, except for reasonable compensation for services rendered in winding up the activities of the limited liability company.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-501 Nature of transferable interest.
----------------------------------------------------------------
A transferable interest is personal property.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(8)(b): executes an assignment for the benefit of creditors; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(8)(c): seeks, consents to, or acquiesces in the appointment of a trustee, receiver, or liquidator of the person or of all or substantially all the person's property;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(9): in the case of a person that is a testamentary or inter vivos trust or is acting as a member by virtue of being a trustee of such a trust, the trust's entire transferable interest in the limited liability company is distributed;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(10): in the case of a person that is an estate or is acting as a member by virtue of being a personal representative of an estate, the estate's entire transferable interest in the limited liability company is distributed, but not merely by reason of substitution of a successor personal representative;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(11): in the case of a person that is not an individual, corporation, unincorporated entity, trust, or estate, the existence of the person terminates;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(12): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication the limited liability company participates in a merger under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(12)(a): the limited liability company is not the surviving entity; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(12)(b): otherwise as a result of the merger, the person ceases to be a member;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(13): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication the limited liability company participates in an interest exchange under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(14): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication the limited liability company participates in a conversion under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(15): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication the limited liability company participates in a domestication under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-602(16): the limited liability company dissolves and completes winding up.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-603 Effect of dissociation.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-603(1): 48-3a-409; 48-3a-504; Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication If a person is dissociated as a member:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-603(1)(a): the person's right to participate as a member in the management and conduct of the company's activities and affairs terminates;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-603(1)(b): 48-3a-409 if the limited liability company is member-managed, the person's duties and obligations under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-603(1)(c): 48-3a-504; Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-603(2): A person's dissociation as a member does not of itself discharge the person from any debt, obligation, or other liability to the limited liability company or the other members which the person incurred while a member.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701 Events causing dissolution.
-----------------------------------------------------------
A limited liability company is dissolved, and its activities and affairs must be wound up, upon the occurrence of any of the following:Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(1): an event, circumstance, or date that the certificate of organization or operating agreement states causes dissolution;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(2): the consent of all the members;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(3): the passage of 90 consecutive days during which the limited liability company has no members unless:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(3)(a): consent to admit at least one specified person as a member is given by transferees owning the rights to receive a majority of distributions as transferees at the time the consent is to be effective; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(3)(b): at least one person becomes a member in accordance with the consent;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(4): upon a petition brought by a member, the entry of a court order dissolving the limited liability company on the grounds that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(4)(a): the conduct of all or substantially all of the limited liability company's activities and affairs is unlawful; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(4)(b): it is not reasonably practicable to carry on the limited liability company's activities and affairs in conformity with the certificate of organization and the operating agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(5): upon a petition brought by a member, the entry of a court order dissolving the limited liability company on the grounds that the managers or those members in control of the limited liability company:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(5)(a): have acted, are acting, or will act in a manner that is illegal or fraudulent; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(5)(b): have acted, are acting, or will act in a manner that is oppressive and was, is, or will be directly harmful to the applicant; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-701(6): 48-3a-708 the signing and filing of a statement of administrative dissolution by the division under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702 Election to purchase in lieu of dissolution.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(1): 48-3a-701(5); (1)
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(1)(a): 48-3a-701(5) In a proceeding under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(1)(b): (1) An election pursuant to this Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(2): 48-3a-701(5)
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(2)(a): 48-3a-701(5) An election to purchase pursuant to this section may be filed with a court at any time within 90 days after the filing of the petition in a proceeding under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(2)(b): If the limited liability company files an election with a court within the 90-day period, or at any later time allowed by the court, to purchase the interest in the limited liability company owned by the applicant member, the limited liability company shall purchase the interest in the manner provided in this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(3)(a): If the limited liability company does not file an election with a court within the time period, but an election to purchase the interest in the limited liability company owned by the applicant member is filed by one or more members within the time period, the limited liability company shall, within 10 days after the later of the end of the time period allowed for the filing of elections to purchase under this section or notification from the court of an election by members to purchase the interest in the limited liability company owned by the applicant member as provided in this section, give written notice of the election to purchase to all members of the limited liability company, other than the applicant member.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(3)(b): The notice shall state the name and the percentage interest in the limited liability company owned by the applicant member and the name and the percentage interest in the limited liability company owned by each electing member.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(3)(c): The notice shall advise any recipients who have not participated in the election of their right to join in the election to purchase the interest in the limited liability company in accordance with this section and of the date by which any notice of intent to participate must be filed with the court.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(4): Members who wish to participate in the purchase of the interest in the limited liability company of the applicant member must file notice of their intention to join in the purchase by electing members no later than 30 days after the effective date of the limited liability company's notice of their right to join in the election to purchase.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(5): All members who have filed with the court an election or notice of their intention to participate in the election to purchase the interest in the limited liability company of the applicant member thereby become irrevocably obligated to participate in the purchase of the interest from the applicant member upon the terms and conditions of this section, unless the court otherwise directs.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(8): (7); 48-3a-701(5); 48-3a-701(5) If the parties are unable to reach an agreement as provided for in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(9):

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-702(9)(b): The terms and conditions may include payment of the purchase price in installments, where necessary in the interest of equity, provision for security to assure payment of the purchase price and any additional costs, fees, and expenses awarded by the court, and an allocation of the interest in the limited liability company among members if the interest in the limited liability company is to be purchased by members.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703 Winding up.
-------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(1): 48-3a-704
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(1)(a): A dissolved limited liability company shall wind up the limited liability company's activities and affairs.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(1)(b): 48-3a-704 Except as otherwise provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2): In winding up the limited liability company's activities and affairs, a limited liability company:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(a): shall discharge the limited liability company's debts, obligations, and other liabilities, settle and close the limited liability company's activities and affairs, and marshal and distribute the assets of the limited liability company; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(b): may:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(b)(i): deliver to the division for filing a statement of dissolution stating the name of the limited liability company and that the limited liability company is dissolved;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(b)(ii): preserve the limited liability company activities, affairs, and property as a going concern for a reasonable time;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(b)(iii): prosecute and defend actions and proceedings, whether civil, criminal, or administrative;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(b)(iv): transfer the limited liability company's property;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(b)(v): settle disputes by mediation or arbitration;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(b)(vi): deliver to the division for filing a statement of termination stating the name of the limited liability company and that the limited liability company is terminated; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(2)(b)(vii): perform other acts necessary or appropriate to the winding up.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(3): 48-3a-407(3); 48-3a-304(1)
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(3)(a): If a dissolved limited liability company has no members, the legal representative of the last person to have been a member may wind up the activities and affairs of the limited liability company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(3)(b): 48-3a-407(3); 48-3a-304(1) If the person does so, the person has the powers of a sole manager under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(4): (3); (4); 48-3a-407(3); 48-3a-304(1) If the legal representative under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(4)(a): 48-3a-407(3); 48-3a-304(1) has the powers of a sole manager under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(4)(b): shall promptly deliver to the division for filing an amendment to the limited liability company's certificate of organization stating:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(4)(b)(i): that the limited liability company has no members;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(4)(b)(ii): the name and street and mailing addresses of the person; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(4)(b)(iii): that the person has been appointed pursuant to this subsection to wind up the limited liability company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(5): (4); 48-3a-701(4); (5) A court may order judicial supervision of the winding up of a dissolved limited liability company, including the appointment of a person to wind up the limited liability company's activities and affairs:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(5)(a): upon a petition by a member if the member establishes good cause;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(5)(b): (4) upon a petition by a transferee if:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(5)(b)(i): the company does not have any members;

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-703(5)(b)(iii): (4) within a reasonable time following the dissolution a person has not been appointed pursuant to Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705 Known claims against dissolved limited liability company.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(1): A dissolved limited liability company in winding up may dispose of the known claims against it by following the procedures described in this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(2): A limited liability company in winding up, electing to dispose of known claims pursuant to this section, may give written notice of the limited liability company's dissolution to known claimants at any time after the effective date of the dissolution.  The written notice must:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(2)(a): describe the information that must be included in a claim;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(2)(b): provide an address to which written notice of any claim must be given to the limited liability company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(2)(c): state the deadline, which may not be fewer than 120 days after the effective date of the notice, by which the dissolved limited liability company must receive the claim; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(2)(d): state that, unless sooner barred by another state statute limiting actions, the claim will be barred if not received by the deadline.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(3): (2) Unless sooner barred by another state statute limiting actions, a claim against the dissolved limited liability company is barred if:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(3)(a): (2) a claimant was given notice under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(3)(b): the dissolved limited liability company delivers to the claimant written notice of rejection of the claim within 90 days after receipt of the claim and the claimant whose claim was rejected by the dissolved limited liability company does not commence a proceeding to enforce the claim within 90 days after the effective date of the rejection notice.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(4): Claims which are not rejected by the dissolved limited liability company in writing within 90 days after receipt of the claim by the dissolved limited liability company shall be considered approved.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(5): (2) The failure of the dissolved limited liability company to give notice to any known claimant pursuant to Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-705(6): This section does not apply to a claim based on an event occurring after the effective date of dissolution or a liability that on that date is contingent.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709 Reinstatement.
----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(1): 48-3a-708; 48-3a-108 A limited liability company that is administratively dissolved under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(1)(a): 48-3a-108 the name of the limited liability company at the time of its administrative dissolution and, if needed, a different name that satisfies Section

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(1)(d): that the grounds for dissolution did not exist or have been cured.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(2): 48-3a-708 A limited liability company administratively dissolved under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(3): 42-2-6.6 A limited liability company retains the limited liability company's name and assumed name, as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(4): To be reinstated, a limited liability company must pay all fees, taxes, interest, and penalties that were due to the division at the time of its administrative dissolution and all fees, taxes, interest, and penalties that would have been due to the division while the limited liability company was administratively dissolved.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(5): If the division determines that an application under Subsection (1) or (2) contains the information required by Subsection (1) or (2), is satisfied that the information is correct, and determines that all payments required to be made to the division by Subsection (4) have been made, the division shall:

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(5)(b): file the statement of reinstatement; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(5)(c): serve a copy of the statement of reinstatement on the limited liability company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(6): When reinstatement under this section is effective, the following rules apply:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(6)(a): The reinstatement relates back to and takes effect as of the effective date of the administrative dissolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(6)(b): The limited liability company may resume its activities and affairs as if the administrative dissolution had not occurred.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-709(6)(c): The rights of a person arising out of an act or omission in reliance on the dissolution before the person knew or had notice of the reinstatement are not affected.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-710 Judicial review of denial of reinstatement.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-710(1): If the division denies a limited liability company's application for reinstatement following administrative dissolution, the division shall serve the limited liability company with a notice in a record that explains the reasons for the denial.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-710(2): A limited liability company may seek judicial review of denial of reinstatement in the district court not later than 30 days after service of the notice of denial.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-802 Derivative action.
--------------------------------------------------
A member may maintain a derivative action to enforce a right of a limited liability company if:Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-802(1): the member first makes a demand on the other members in a member-managed limited liability company, or the managers of a manager-managed limited liability company, requesting that they cause the limited liability company to bring an action to enforce the right, and the managers or other members do not bring the action within a reasonable time; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-802(2): (1) a demand under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-803 Proper plaintiff.
-------------------------------------------------
A derivative action to enforce a right of a limited liability company may be maintained only by a person that is a member at the time the action is commenced and:Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-803(1): was a member when the conduct giving rise to the action occurred; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-803(2): whose status as a member devolved on the person by operation of law or pursuant to the terms of the operating agreement from a person that was a member at the time of the conduct.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-804 Pleading.
-----------------------------------------
In a derivative action, the complaint must state with particularity:Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-804(1): the date and content of plaintiff's demand and the response by the managers or other members to the demand; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-804(2): why the demand should be excused as futile.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805 Special litigation committee.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(1): (1); 48-3a-410 If a limited liability company is named as or made a party in a derivative proceeding, the limited liability company may appoint a special litigation committee to investigate the claims asserted in the proceeding and determine whether pursuing the action is in the best interests of the limited liability company.  If the limited liability company appoints a special litigation committee, on motion by the committee made in the name of the limited liability company, except for good cause shown, the court shall stay discovery for the time reasonably necessary to permit the committee to make its investigation.  This Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(1)(a): 48-3a-410 enforcing a person's right to information under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(1)(b): granting extraordinary relief in the form of a temporary restraining order or preliminary injunction upon a showing of good cause.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(2): A special litigation committee must be composed of one or more disinterested and independent individuals, who may be members.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(3): A special litigation committee may be appointed:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(3)(a): in a member-managed limited liability company:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(3)(a)(i): by the consent of a majority of the members not named as parties in the proceeding; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(3)(a)(ii): if all members are named as parties in the proceeding, by a majority of the members named as defendants; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(3)(b): in a manager-managed limited liability company:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(3)(b)(i): by a majority of the managers not named as parties in the proceeding; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(3)(b)(ii): if all managers are named as parties in the proceeding, by a majority of the managers named as defendants.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(4): After appropriate investigation, a special litigation committee may determine that it is in the best interests of the limited liability company that the proceeding:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(4)(a): continue under the control of the plaintiff;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(4)(b): continue under the control of the committee;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(4)(c): be settled on terms approved by the committee; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(4)(d): be dismissed.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-805(5): (4); (1) After making a determination under Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-806 Proceeds and expenses.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-806(1): (2) Except as otherwise provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-806(1)(a): any proceeds or other benefits of a derivative action, whether by judgment, compromise, or settlement, belong to the limited liability company and not to the plaintiff; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-806(1)(b): if the plaintiff receives any proceeds, the plaintiff shall remit them immediately to the limited liability company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-806(2): If a derivative action is successful in whole or in part, the court may award the plaintiff reasonable expenses, including reasonable attorney's fees and costs, from the recovery of the limited liability company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-806(3): A derivative action on behalf of a limited liability company may not be voluntarily dismissed or settled without the court's approval.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901 Governing law.
----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901(1): The law of the jurisdiction of formation of a foreign limited liability company governs:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901(1)(a): the internal affairs of the foreign limited liability company; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901(1)(b): the liability of a member as member and a manager as manager for a debt, obligation, or other liability of the company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901(2): A foreign limited liability company is not precluded from registering to do business in this state because of any difference between the law of the jurisdiction of formation and the law of this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901(3): Registration of a foreign limited liability company to do business in this state does not authorize the foreign limited liability company to engage in any activities or affairs or exercise any power that a limited liability company may not engage in or exercise in this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901(4)(a): The division may permit a tribal limited liability company to apply for authority to transact business in the state in the same manner as a foreign limited liability company formed in another state.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-901(4)(b): If a tribal limited liability company elects to apply for authority to transact business in the state, for purposes of this chapter, the tribal limited liability company shall be treated in the same manner as a foreign limited liability company formed under the laws of another state.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-902 Registration to do business in this state.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-902(1): A foreign limited liability company may not do business in this state until it registers with the division under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-902(2): A foreign limited liability company doing business in this state may not maintain an action or proceeding in this state unless it is registered to do business in this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-902(3): The failure of a foreign limited liability company to register to do business in this state does not impair the validity of a contract or act of the foreign limited liability company or preclude it from defending an action or proceeding in this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-902(4): A limitation on the liability of a member or manager of a foreign limited liability company is not waived solely because the foreign limited liability company does business in this state without registering to do business in this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-902(5): 48-3a-901(1); (2) Subsections


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-903 Foreign registration statement.
---------------------------------------------------------------
To register to do business in this state, a foreign limited liability company must deliver a foreign registration statement to the division for filing.  The statement must state:Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-903(1): 48-3a-108; 48-3a-906(1) the name of the foreign limited liability company and, if the name does not comply with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-903(2): that the company is a foreign limited liability company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-903(3): the name of the foreign limited liability company's jurisdiction of formation;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-903(4): the street and mailing addresses of the foreign limited liability company's principal office and, if the law of the jurisdiction of formation requires the foreign limited liability company to maintain an office in that jurisdiction, the street and mailing addresses of the required office; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-903(5): 16-17-203(1) the information required by Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-904 Amendment of foreign registration statement.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
A registered foreign limited liability company shall deliver to the division for filing an amendment to its foreign registration statement if there is a change in:Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-904(1): the name of the foreign limited liability company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-904(2): the foreign limited liability company's jurisdiction of formation;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-904(3): 48-3a-903(4) an address required by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-904(4): 48-3a-903(5) the information required by Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905 Activities not constituting doing business.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1): Activities of a foreign limited liability company which do not constitute doing business in this state under this part include:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(a): maintaining, defending, mediating, arbitrating, or settling an action or proceeding;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(b): carrying on any activity concerning its internal affairs, including holding meetings of its members or managers;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(c): maintaining accounts in financial institutions;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(d): maintaining offices or agencies for the transfer, exchange, and registration of the securities of the foreign limited liability company or maintaining trustees or depositories with respect to those securities;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(e): selling through independent contractors;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(f): soliciting or obtaining orders by any means if the orders require acceptance outside this state before they become contracts;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(g): creating or acquiring indebtedness, mortgages, or security interests in property;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(h): securing or collecting debts or enforcing mortgages or security interests in property securing the debts and holding, protecting, or maintaining property;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(i): conducting an isolated transaction that is not in the course of similar transactions;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(j): owning, without more, property; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(1)(k): doing business in interstate commerce.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(2): A person does not do business in this state solely by being a member or manager of a foreign limited liability company that does business in this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-905(3): This section does not apply in determining the contacts or activities that may subject a foreign limited liability company to service of process, taxation, or regulation under law of this state other than this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-906 Noncomplying name of foreign limited liability company.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-906(1): 48-3a-108; 48-3a-108; (1); Title 42, Chapter 2, Conducting Business Under Assumed Name; Title 42, Chapter 2, Conducting Business Under Assumed Name A foreign limited liability company whose name does not comply with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-906(1)(a): the alternate name;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-906(1)(b): the foreign limited liability company's name, with the addition of its jurisdiction of formation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-906(1)(c): Title 42, Chapter 2, Conducting Business Under Assumed Name an assumed or fictitious name the foreign limited liability company is authorized to use under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-906(2): 48-3a-108; (1); 48-3a-108 If a registered foreign limited liability company changes its name to one that does not comply with Section


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-907 Withdrawal deemed on conversion to domestic filing entity or domestic limited liability partnership.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
A registered foreign limited liability company that converts to a domestic limited liability partnership or to a domestic entity that is organized, incorporated, or otherwise formed through the delivery of a record to the division for filing is deemed to have withdrawn its registration on the effective date of the conversion.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908 Withdrawal on dissolution or conversion to nonfiling entity other than limited liability partnership.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1): (2) A registered foreign limited liability company that has dissolved and completed winding up or has converted to a domestic or foreign entity that is not organized, incorporated, or otherwise formed through the public filing of a record, other than a limited liability partnership, shall deliver a statement of withdrawal to the division for filing.  The statement must state:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1)(a): in the case of a foreign limited liability company that has completed winding up:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1)(a)(i): its name and jurisdiction of formation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1)(a)(ii): that the foreign limited liability company surrenders its registration to do business in this state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1)(b): (2) in the case of a foreign limited liability company that has converted:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1)(b)(i): the name of the converting foreign limited liability company and its jurisdiction of formation;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1)(b)(ii): the type of entity to which the foreign limited liability company has converted and its jurisdiction of formation;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1)(b)(iii): that the converted entity surrenders the converting foreign limited liability company's registration to do business in this state and revokes the authority of the converting foreign limited liability company's registered agent to act as registered agent in this state on behalf of the foreign limited liability company or the converted entity; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(1)(b)(iv): (2) a mailing address to which service of process may be made under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-908(2): 16-17-301(2) After a withdrawal under this section of a foreign limited liability company that has converted to another type of entity is effective, service of process in any action or proceeding based on a cause of action arising during the time the foreign limited liability company was registered to do business in this state may be made pursuant to Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909 Transfer of registration.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909(1): 48-3a-108; 48-3a-906(1); 16-17-203(1) When a registered foreign limited liability company has merged into a foreign entity that is not registered to do business in this state or has converted to a foreign entity required to register with the division to do business in this state, the foreign entity shall deliver to the division for filing an application for transfer of registration.  The application must state:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909(1)(a): the name of the registered foreign limited liability company before the merger or conversion;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909(1)(b): that before the merger or conversion the registration pertained to a foreign limited liability company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909(1)(c): 48-3a-108; 48-3a-906(1) the name of the applicant foreign entity into which the foreign limited liability company has merged or to which it has been converted, and, if the name does not comply with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909(1)(d): the type of entity of the applicant foreign entity and its jurisdiction of formation;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909(1)(e): the street and mailing addresses of the principal office of the applicant foreign entity and, if the law of the entity's jurisdiction of formation requires the entity to maintain an office in that jurisdiction, the street and mailing addresses of that office; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909(1)(f): 16-17-203(1) the information required under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-909(2): When an application for transfer of registration takes effect, the registration of the foreign limited liability company to do business in this state is transferred without interruption to the foreign entity into which the foreign company has merged or to which it has been converted.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-910 Termination of registration.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-911 Withdrawal of registration of registered foreign limited liability company.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-911(1): (2) A registered foreign limited liability company may withdraw its registration by delivering a statement of withdrawal to the division for filing.  The statement of withdrawal must state:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-911(1)(a): the name of the foreign limited liability company and its jurisdiction of formation;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-911(1)(b): that the foreign limited liability company is not doing business in this state and that it withdraws its registration to do business in this state;
