Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204 Series related provisions in operating agreement.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(1): An operating agreement may provide for classes or groups of members or managers associated with a series having such relative rights, powers, and duties as the operating agreement may provide.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(2): The operating agreement may provide for the future creation of additional classes or groups of members or managers associated with the series having such relative rights, powers, and duties as may from time to time be established, including rights, powers, and duties senior to existing classes and groups of members or managers associated with the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(3): An operating agreement may provide for the taking of an action, including the amendment of the operating agreement, without the vote or approval of any member or manager or class or group of members or managers, including all action to create under the provisions of the operating agreement a class or group of the series of membership interests that was not previously outstanding.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(4): An operating agreement may provide that any member or class or group of members associated with a series does not have voting rights.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(5): An operating agreement may grant to all or certain identified members or managers or a specified class or group of the members or managers associated with a series the right to vote on any matter separately or with all or any class or group of the members or managers associated with the series.  Voting by members or managers associated with a series may be on any basis including:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(5)(a): a per capita basis;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(5)(b): a number basis;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(5)(c): on the basis of a financial interest; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1204(5)(d): by class or group.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205 Management of a series.
--------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(1): A series is member-managed unless the operating agreement:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(1)(a): expressly provides that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(1)(a)(i): the series is or will be "manager-managed";
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(1)(a)(ii): the series is or will be "managed by managers"; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(1)(a)(iii): management of the series is or will be "vested in managers"; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(1)(b): includes words of similar import.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(2): 48-3a-1204 In a member-managed series, unless modified pursuant to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(2)(a): The management and conduct of the series are vested in the members of the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(2)(b): Each series member has equal rights in the management and conduct of the series' activities.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(2)(c): A difference arising among series members as to a matter in the ordinary course of the activities of the series shall be decided by a majority of the series members.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(2)(d): An act outside the ordinary course of the activities of the series may be undertaken only with the consent of all members of the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(2)(e): The operating agreement may be amended only with the consent of all members of the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3): 48-3a-1204; Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication In a manager-managed series, the following rules apply:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(a): Except as otherwise expressly provided in this chapter, any matter relating to the activities of the series is decided exclusively by the managers of the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(b): Each series manager has equal rights in the management and conduct of the activities of the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(c): A difference arising among managers of a series as to a matter in the ordinary course of the activities of the series shall be decided by a majority of the managers of the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(d): 48-3a-1204; Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication Unless modified pursuant to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(d)(i): sell, lease, exchange, or otherwise dispose of all, or substantially all, of the series' property, with or without the goodwill, outside the ordinary course of the series' activities;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(d)(ii): Part 10, Merger, Interest Exchange, Conversion, and Domestication approve a transaction under
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(d)(iii): undertake any other act outside the ordinary course of the series' activities; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(d)(iv): amend the operating agreement as it pertains to the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(e): A manager of the series may be chosen at any time by the consent of a majority of the members of the series and remains a manager of the series until a successor has been chosen, unless the series manager at an earlier time resigns, is removed, or dies, or, in the case of a series manager that is not an individual, terminates.  A series manager may be removed at any time by the consent of a majority of the members without notice or cause.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(f): A person need not be a series member to be a manager of a series, but the dissociation of a series member that is also a series manager removes the person as a manager of the series.  If a person that is both a series manager and a series member ceases to be a manager of the series, that cessation does not by itself dissociate the person as a member of the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(3)(g): A person's ceasing to be a series manager does not discharge any debt, obligation, or other liability to the series or members of the series which the person incurred while a manager of the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(4): An action requiring the consent of members of a series under this chapter may be taken without a meeting, and a member of a series may appoint a proxy or other agent to consent or otherwise act for the series member by signing an appointing record, personally or by the series member's agent.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(5): The dissolution of a series does not affect the applicability of this section.  However, a person that wrongfully causes dissolution of the series loses the right to participate in management as a series member and a series manager.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1205(6): This chapter does not entitle a member of a series to remuneration for services performed for a member-managed series, except for reasonable compensation for services rendered in winding up the activities of the series.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206 Series distributions.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(1): 48-3a-502; 48-3a-503 Any distribution made by a series before its dissolution and winding up must be in equal shares among the series members and dissociated series members, except to the extent necessary to comply with any transfer effective under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(2): A person has a right to a distribution before the dissolution and winding up of a series only if the series decides to make an interim distribution.  A person's dissociation with respect to a series does not entitle the person to a distribution.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(3): 48-3a-711(3) A person does not have a right to demand or receive a distribution from a series in any form other than money.  Except as otherwise provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(4): If a series member or transferee becomes entitled to receive a distribution, the series member or transferee has the status of, and is entitled to all remedies available to, a creditor of the series with respect to the distribution.  However, the series' obligation to make a distribution is subject to offset for any amounts owed to the series by the member or a person dissociated as a member on whose account the distribution is made.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(5): A series may not make a distribution if after the distribution:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(5)(a): the series would not be able to pay its debts as they become due in the ordinary course of the series' activities; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(5)(b): the series' total assets would be less than the sum of its total liabilities plus the amount that would be needed, if the series were to be dissolved, wound up, and terminated at the time of the distribution, to satisfy the preferential rights upon dissolution, winding up, and termination of members whose preferential rights are superior to those of persons receiving the distribution.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(6): (5) A series may base a determination that a distribution is not prohibited under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(7): (9); (5) Except as otherwise provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(7)(a): in the case of a distribution by purchase, redemption, or other acquisition of a transferable interest in the series, as of the date money or other property is transferred or debt incurred by the series; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(7)(b): in all other cases, as of the date:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(7)(b)(i): the distribution is authorized, if the payment occurs within 120 days after that date; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(7)(b)(ii): the payment is made, if the payment occurs more than 120 days after the distribution is authorized.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(8): A series' indebtedness to a series member incurred by reason of a distribution made in accordance with this section is at parity with the series' indebtedness to its general, unsecured creditors.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(9): (5) A series' indebtedness, including indebtedness issued in connection with or as part of a distribution, is not a liability for purposes of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(10): (11); 48-3a-409 Except as otherwise provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(11): (10) To the extent the operating agreement of a member-managed series expressly relieves a series member of the authority and responsibility to consent to distributions and imposes that authority and responsibility on one or more other members of the series, the liability stated in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(12): A person that receives a distribution from a series knowing that the distribution to that person was made in violation of this section is personally liable to the limited liability company but only to the extent that the distribution received by the person exceeded the amount that could have been properly paid under this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(13): (10); (10); (12); (12) A person against which an action is commenced because the person is liable under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(13)(a): (10) implead any other person that is liable under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(13)(b): (12); (12) implead any person that received a distribution in violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1206(14): An action under this section is barred if not commenced within two years after the distribution.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1207 Events causing dissociation from a series.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1207(1): Unless otherwise provided in the operating agreement, a member ceases to be associated with a series and to have the power to exercise a right or power of a member with respect to the series upon the assignment of all of the member's transferable interest in the limited liability company with respect to the series.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1207(2): Unless otherwise provided in an operating agreement, an event under this chapter or the operating agreement that causes a member to cease to be associated with a series does not, by itself:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1207(2)(a): cause the member to cease to be associated with another series;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1207(2)(b): terminate the continued membership of a member in the limited liability company; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1207(2)(c): cause the termination of the series, regardless of whether the member is the last remaining member associated with the series.

---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1208(1): Except to the extent otherwise provided in the operating agreement, a series may be dissolved and its affairs wound up without causing the dissolution of the limited liability company.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1208(4)(c)(i): own more than 50% of the transferable interests of the series owned by members associated with the series who have not wrongfully caused the dissolution of the series; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1208(4)(c)(ii): own more than 50% of the transferable interests of each class or group associated with the series owned by members associated with the series who have not wrongfully caused the dissolution of the series.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1209 Foreign limited liability company -- Series.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
A foreign limited liability company that is registered to do business in this state that is governed by an operating agreement that establishes or provides for the establishment of a series of transferable interests having separate rights, powers, or duties with respect to specified property or obligations of the foreign limited liability company, or profits and losses associated with the specified property or obligations, shall indicate that fact on the foreign registration statement filed by the division.  In addition, the foreign limited liability company shall state on the foreign registration statement whether the debts, liabilities, and obligations incurred, contracted for, or otherwise existing with respect to a particular series, if any, are enforceable against the assets of such series only, and not against the assets of the foreign limited liability company generally or any other series.  Notice in a foreign limited liability company's foreign registration statement of the limitation on liability of a series as referenced in this section shall have the same effect found in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1301 Application of this part.
----------------------------------------------------------
If a conflict arises between this part and another provision of this chapter, this part controls.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1401 Uniformity of application and construction.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------
In applying and construing this chapter, consideration must be given to the need to promote uniformity of the law with respect to its subject matter among states that enact the uniform act upon which this chapter is based.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1402 Severability clause.
-----------------------------------------------------
If any provision of this chapter or its application to any person or circumstance is held invalid, the invalidity does not affect other provisions or applications of this chapter which can be given effect without the invalid provision or application, and to this end the provisions of this chapter are severable.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1403 Relation to Electronic Signatures in Global and National Commerce Act.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
This chapter modifies, limits, and supersedes the Electronic Signatures in Global and National Commerce Act, 15 U.S.C. Sec. 7001 et seq., but does not modify, limit, or supersede Section 101(c) of that act, 15 U.S.C. Sec. 7001(c), or authorize electronic delivery of any of the notices described in Section 103(b) of that act, 15 U.S.C. Sec. 7003(b).

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1404 Savings clause.
------------------------------------------------
This chapter does not affect an action commenced, proceeding brought, or right accrued before this chapter takes effect.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405 Application to existing relationships.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(1): Before January 1, 2016, this chapter governs only:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(1)(a): a limited liability company formed on or after January 1, 2014; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(1)(b): except as otherwise provided in Subsection (3), a limited liability company formed before January 1, 2014, which elects, in the manner provided in its operating agreement or by law for amending the operating agreement, to be subject to this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(2): Except as otherwise provided in Subsection (3), on and after January 1, 2016, this chapter governs all limited liability companies.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(3): 48-3a-102; 48-3a-114 For the purposes of applying this chapter to a limited liability company formed before January 1, 2014:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(3)(a): the limited liability company's articles of organization are deemed to be the limited liability company's certificate of organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(3)(b): 48-3a-102; 48-3a-114 for the purposes of applying Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(3)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(3)(c)(i): the limited liability company has perpetual duration unless otherwise stated in the limited liability company's articles of organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-3a-1405(3)(c)(ii): after the limited liability company's duration ends in accordance with the articles of organization, the limited liability company is dissolved, and its activities and affairs must be wound up.


Utah Code Annotated - Title 48 - Chapter 4 - Benefit Limited Liability Company Act
**********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-101 Title.
-------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Benefit Limited Liability Company Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102 Application and effect of chapter.
-----------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102(1): This chapter applies to a benefit company organized under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102(2)(a): The existence of a provision in this chapter does not itself create an implication that a contrary or different rule of law is applicable to a limited liability company that is not a benefit company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102(2)(b): This chapter does not affect a statute or rule of law that is applicable to a limited liability company that is not a benefit company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102(3): Title 48, Chapter 3a, Utah Revised Uniform Limited Liability Company Act; Title 48, Chapter 3a, Utah Revised Uniform Limited Liability Company Act
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102(3)(a): Title 48, Chapter 3a, Utah Revised Uniform Limited Liability Company Act Except as otherwise provided in this chapter,
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102(3)(b): Title 48, Chapter 3a, Utah Revised Uniform Limited Liability Company Act The provisions of this chapter control over any inconsistent provision of
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-102(4): The operating agreement of a benefit company may not limit, be inconsistent with, or supersede a provision of this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103 Definitions.
-------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(1): "Benefit company" means a limited liability company:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(1)(a): that elects to become subject to this chapter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(1)(b): the status of which as a benefit company has not been terminated.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(2): "Benefit enforcement proceeding" means a proceeding in a court of competent jurisdiction for:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(2)(a): failure of a benefit company to pursue or create general public benefit or a specific public benefit described in the benefit company's certificate of organization; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(2)(b): a violation of an obligation, duty, or standard of conduct under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(3): "General public benefit" means a material positive impact on society and the environment:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(3)(a): taken as a whole;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(3)(b): assessed against a third-party standard; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(3)(c): from the business of a benefit company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(4): "Immediate family member" means a parent, spouse, surviving spouse, child, or sibling.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(5): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(5)(a): "Independent person" means a person who has no material relationship with a benefit company or a subsidiary of the benefit company.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(5)(b): "Independent person" does not include a person:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(5)(b)(i): who is, or has been within the last three years, an employee of the benefit company or a subsidiary of the benefit company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(5)(b)(ii): whose immediate family member is, or has been within the last three years, an executive officer of the benefit company or a subsidiary of the benefit company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(5)(b)(iii): who owns 5% or more of the outstanding interests of the benefit company, calculated as if all outstanding rights to acquire interests in the benefit company have been exercised; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(5)(b)(iv): who owns 5% or more of the outstanding interests in an entity, calculated as if all outstanding rights to acquire interests in the entity have been exercised, that owns 5% or more of the outstanding interests of the benefit company, calculated as if all outstanding rights to acquire interests in the benefit company have been exercised.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(6): (6)(b)(i) "Minimum status vote" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(6)(a): in the case of a limited liability company, in addition to any other required approval or vote, the satisfaction of the following conditions:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(6)(a)(i): the members of every class or series may vote as a separate voting group on an action of the limited liability company regardless of a limitation state in the certificate of organization or operating agreement on the voting rights of any class or series; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(6)(a)(ii): the action of the limited liability company is required to be approved by vote of the members of each class or series entitled to cast at least two-thirds of the votes that all members of the class or series are entitled to cast on the action; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(6)(b): (6)(b)(i) in the case of a domestic entity other than a limited liability company, in addition to any other required approval, vote, or consent, the satisfaction of the following conditions:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(6)(b)(i): the holders of every class or series of interest in the entity that are entitled to receive a distribution of any kind from the entity may vote on or consent to the action regardless of any otherwise applicable limitation on voting or consent rights of the class or series; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(6)(b)(ii): (6)(b)(i) the action of the limited liability company is required to be approved by vote or consent of the holders described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(7): "Owns" includes ownership as the owner of record or as a beneficial owner.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(8): "Specific public benefit" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(8)(a): providing low-income or underserved individuals or communities with beneficial products or services;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(8)(b): promoting economic opportunity for individuals or communities beyond the creation of jobs in the normal course of business;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(8)(c): protecting or restoring the environment;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(8)(d): improving human health;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(8)(e): promoting the arts, sciences, or advancement of knowledge;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(8)(f): increasing the flow of capital to entities with a purpose to benefit society or the environment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(8)(g): conferring any other particular benefit on society or the environment.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(9): "Subsidiary" means, in relation to a person, an entity in which the person owns beneficially or of record, 50% or more of the outstanding equity interests, calculated as if all outstanding rights to acquire equity interests in the entity have been exercised.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10): 48-4-301(1)(a)(ii); (v); (10)(b)(ii); (10)(b)(vi)(A) "Third-party standard" means a standard for defining, reporting, and assessing overall social and environmental performance that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(a): 48-4-301(1)(a)(ii); (v) assesses the effect of a business and a business's operations on the interests described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b): (10)(b)(ii); (10)(b)(vi)(A) is developed by an entity:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(i): that is independent of the benefit company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(ii): whose governing body is comprised of no more than one-third of members who are representatives of any of the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(ii)(A): an association of businesses that operate in a specific industry whose members are measured by the standard;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(ii)(B): businesses from a specific industry or an association of businesses in that industry; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(ii)(C): businesses whose performance is assessed against the standard;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(iii): (10)(b)(ii) that is not materially financed by an association or business described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(iv): that has access to necessary expertise to assess overall social and environmental performance;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(v): uses a balanced multistakeholder approach to develop the standard, including a public comment period of at least 30 days; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(vi): (10)(b)(vi)(A) makes the following information publically available:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(vi)(A): the criteria considered when measuring the overall social and environmental performance of a business;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(vi)(B): (10)(b)(vi)(A) the relative weightings, if any, of the criteria described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(vi)(C): the identity of each director, officer, material owner, and governing body of the entity that developed and controls revisions to the standard;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(vi)(D): the process by which revisions to the standard and changes to the membership of the governing body are made; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-103(10)(b)(vi)(E): an accounting of the revenue and sources of financial support for the entity, with sufficient detail to disclose a relationship that could reasonably be considered to present a potential conflict of interest.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301 Standard of conduct for members.
---------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1): When discharging a duty under this chapter, each member of a member-managed benefit company:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(a): shall consider the effect of any action or inaction on:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(a)(i): the members of the benefit company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(a)(ii): the employees and workforce of the benefit company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(a)(iii): the interests of customers as beneficiaries of the benefit company's general public benefit purpose or specific public benefit purpose;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(a)(iv): community and societal considerations, including those of each community in which offices or facilities of the benefit company or the benefit company's subsidiaries or suppliers are located;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(a)(v): the local and global environment;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(a)(vi): the short-term and long-term interests of the benefit company, including benefits that may accrue to the benefit company from the benefit company's long-term plans and the possibility that the interests may be best served by the continued independence of the benefit company; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(a)(vii): the ability of the benefit company to accomplish the benefit company's general public benefit purpose and any specific public benefit purpose; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(1)(b): may consider other pertinent factors or the interests of any other group that the member considers appropriate.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(2): (1)(a); (b) A member is not required to prioritize the interests of a person or factor described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(3): (1); (2); 48-3a-409 A member's consideration of interests and factors in accordance with Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-301(4): A member of a member-managed limited liability company that is a benefit company does not have a duty to a person who is a beneficiary of the benefit company's general public benefit purpose or a specific public benefit purpose arising from the person's status as a beneficiary.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-302 Standard of conduct for managers and officers.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-302(1): 48-4-301(1); (2) Each manager of a manager-managed benefit company shall consider the interests and factors described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-302(2): 48-4-301(1); (2) If a benefit company has a person serving as an officer, the person shall consider the interests and factors described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-302(2)(a): the officer has discretion to act with respect to the matter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-302(2)(b): it reasonably appears to the officer that the matter may have a material effect on the benefit company's creation of a general public benefit or a specific public benefit identified in the benefit company's certificate of organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-302(3): 48-4-301(1); (2); 48-3a-409 A manager's consideration of the interests and factors described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-302(4): A manager or officer does not have a duty to a person who is a beneficiary of the benefit company's general public benefit purpose or a specific public benefit purpose arising from the person's status as a beneficiary.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303 Right of action.
-----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(1): Except in a benefit enforcement proceeding, a person may not bring an action or assert a claim against a benefit company or a benefit company's member, manager, or officer with respect to:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(1)(a): failure to pursue or create general public benefit or a specific public benefit set forth in the benefit company's certificate of organization; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(1)(b): violation of a duty or standard of conduct under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(2): A benefit company is not liable for monetary damages under this chapter for a failure of the benefit company to pursue or create general public benefit or a specific public benefit.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(3): Only the following may commence or maintain a benefit enforcement proceeding:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(3)(a): the benefit company, directly; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(3)(b): one or more of the following, derivatively:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(3)(b)(i): a member that owned at least 2% of the total number of interests of a class or series outstanding at the time of the act or omission complained of;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(3)(b)(ii): a manager of a manager-managed benefit company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(3)(b)(iii): a person or group of persons who own beneficially or of record at least 5% of the interests in an association of which the benefit company is a subsidiary at the time of the act or omission complained of; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-303(3)(b)(iv): any person or group of persons specified in the benefit company's certificate of organization or operating agreement.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401 Annual benefit report.
-----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1): A benefit company shall prepare an annual benefit report that includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(a): a narrative description of:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(a)(i): the ways in which the benefit company pursued the benefit company's general public benefit purpose during the year and the extent to which general public benefit was created;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(a)(ii): the ways in which the benefit company pursued any specific public benefit that the benefit company's certificate of organization states is the purpose of the benefit company to create and the extent to which the specific public benefit was created;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(a)(iii): any circumstances that have hindered the benefit company's creation of general public benefit or any specific public benefit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(a)(iv): the process and rationale for selecting or changing the third-party standard used to prepare the benefit report;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(b): an assessment of the overall social and environmental performance of the benefit company against a third-party standard:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(b)(i): applied consistently with any application of the standard in prior benefit reports; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(b)(ii): accompanied by an explanation of the reasons for any inconsistent application; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(1)(c): any connection between the organization that established the third-party standard, or the organization's directors or officers, or a holder of 5% or more of the governance interests in the organization, and the benefit company or the benefit company's members, managers, or officers or any holder of 5% or more of the outstanding interests in the benefit company, including any financial or governance relationship that might materially affect the credibility of the use of the third-party standard.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-4-401(2): (1)(b) The assessment described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated - Title 48 - Chapter 5 - Decentralized Autonomous Organization Act
**************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101 Definitions.
-------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(1): "Administrator" means a person that is appointed in a manner specified in the by-laws to make decisions for specific, predefined operations of the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(2): "Asset" means an item of value, whether on-chain or off-chain.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(3): "By-laws" means the procedural rules and regulations that govern a decentralized autonomous organization and the interaction of the decentralized autonomous organization's members and participants.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(4): "Cryptographic proof" means a mathematical proof that verifies that a message has not been tampered with or altered in any way and can be verified by a person that has access to the original message and the proof.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(5): "Decentralized" means that decision-making is distributed among multiple persons.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(6): "Decentralized autonomous organization" means an organization:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(6)(a): created by one or more smart contracts;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(6)(b): that implements rules enabling individuals to coordinate for decentralized governance of an organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(6)(c): that is an entity formed under this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(7): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(7)(a): "Developer" means a person involved in the development or maintenance of a decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(7)(b): "Developer" includes a person that provides:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(7)(b)(i): software code; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(7)(b)(ii): design, business, legal, or ancillary support.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(8): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(8)(a): "Dispute resolution mechanism" means an on-chain alternative dispute resolution system that enables persons to resolve disputes arising out of a decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(8)(b): "Dispute resolution mechanism" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(8)(b)(i): arbitration;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(8)(b)(ii): expert determination; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(8)(b)(iii): an on-chain alternative court system.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(9): "Division" means the Division of Corporations and Commercial Code.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(10): "Failure event" means an error in the decentralized autonomous organization's software code or an exploit that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(10)(a): renders the decentralized autonomous organization inoperative; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(10)(b): fundamentally changes the expected operation of the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(11): "Graphical user interface" means a publicly accessible interface through which a person interacts with computer software through visual indicator representations.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(12): "Hard fork" means a blockchain software upgrade that is not compatible with previous versions of the blockchain software and requires all users to upgrade to the latest version of the blockchain software.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(13): "Legal representative" means an individual appointed in the manner specified in the by-laws of a decentralized autonomous organization to perform procedural functions off-chain on behalf of a decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(14): "Majority chain" means the version of the blockchain accepted by more than half of the blockchain's validators following a hard fork.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(15): "Meeting" means a synchronous or asynchronous event for the purpose of discussing and acting upon decentralized autonomous organization related matters by members or participants.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(16): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(16)(a): "Member" means a person who has governance rights in a decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(16)(b): "Member" does not include an individual that has involuntarily received a token with governance rights, unless that person has chosen to participate in governance by undertaking a governance behavior, on-chain or off-chain, for the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(17): "Minority chain" means the version of the chain that is not the majority chain following a hard fork.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(18): "Off-chain" means any action that is not on-chain.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(19): "On-chain" means any action that is recorded and verified on a blockchain.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(20): "On-chain contribution" refers to any token segregated and locked in one of the decentralized autonomous organization's smart contracts for the purpose of member buy-in to the decentralized autonomous organization and the provision of withdrawable capital.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(21): 48-5-201 "Organizer" means a person that submits the certificate of filing as required in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(22): "Participant" means a person that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(22)(a): is not a member of a decentralized autonomous organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(22)(b): holds or interacts with a token of a decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(23): "Permissionless blockchain" means a publicly distributed ledger that allows a person to transact and produce blocks in accordance with the blockchain protocol, in which the validity of the block is independent of the identity of the user.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(24): "Public address" means a unique, durable identifier that an individual can transact with on a permissionless blockchain.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(25): "Public forum" means a freely accessible online environment that is commonly used for the exercise of speech and public debate.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(26): "Public signal" means a declaration authorized by the decentralized autonomous organization in a public forum.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(27): "Quality assurance" means a security review of the software code of the decentralized autonomous organization in accordance with industry standards.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(28): "Redeem" means to exchange a token for the value that the token represents.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(29): "Smart contract" means software code that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(29)(a): is deployed on a permissionless blockchain;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(29)(b): consists of a set of predefined instructions executed in a distributed manner by the nodes of an underlying blockchain network; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(29)(c): produces a change on the blockchain network.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(30): "Token" means a record on a permissionless blockchain that represents an asset, participation right, or other entitlement.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-101(31): "Transaction" means a new entry in a permissionless blockchain, including the recording of a change in ownership of an asset or participation in a decentralized autonomous organization.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-102 Governing document hierarchy -- Governing law.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
A decentralized autonomous organization shall be governed by the following, listed in order of primacy:Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-102(1): this act;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-102(2): the by-laws of the decentralized autonomous organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-102(3): Chapter 3a, Utah Revised Uniform Limited Liability Company Act if this act and a decentralized autonomous organization's by-laws are silent, the provisions of
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-102(4): principles of law and equity.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-103 Powers of the division.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-103(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-103(1)(a): The division may make, amend, or rescind a rule, form, or order when necessary to carry out this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-103(1)(b): The division shall make rules in accordance with Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-103(2): 48-5-201 The division may by rule:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-103(2)(a): provide the form and content of a registration requirement required under this chapter;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-103(2)(b): 48-5-201 provide the method of determining whether formation requirements described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-103(2)(c): identify industry standards for determining whether the decentralized autonomous organization has undergone security review for quality assurance.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-104 Legal personality.
-------------------------------------------------
A decentralized autonomous organization that meets the requirements of this act:Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-104(1): shall be deemed a legal entity separate and distinct from the decentralized autonomous organization's members;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-104(2): has the capacity to sue and be sued in the decentralized autonomous organization's own name and the power to do all things necessary or convenient to carry on the decentralized autonomous organization's activities and affairs;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-104(3): shall meet the decentralized autonomous organization's liabilities through the decentralized autonomous organization's assets;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-104(4): may have any lawful purpose; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-104(5): has perpetual duration.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105 Permitted names.
-----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(1)(a): The name of a limited liability decentralized autonomous organization shall contain the words limited liability decentralized autonomous organization or limited decentralized autonomous organization or the abbreviation L.L.D., LLD, L.D., or LD.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(1)(b): Limited may be abbreviated as Ltd., and decentralized autonomous organization may be abbreviated as DAO.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(2): Except as authorized by Subsection (3), the name of a decentralized autonomous organization shall be distinguishable as defined in Subsection (4) upon the records of the division from:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(2)(a): the actual name, reserved name, or fictitious or assumed name of any entity registered with the division; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(2)(b): any tradename, trademark, or service mark registered with the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(3): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(3)(a): A decentralized autonomous organization may apply to the division for approval to reserve a name that is not distinguishable upon the division's records from one or more of the names described in Subsection (2).
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(3)(b): The division shall approve the name for which the decentralized autonomous organization applies under Subsection (3)(a) if:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(3)(b)(i): the other person with a name that is not distinguishable from the name under which the applicant desires to file:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(3)(b)(i)(A): consents to the filing in writing; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(3)(b)(i)(B): files a form approved by the division to change the person's name to a name that is distinguishable from the name of the applicant; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(3)(b)(ii): the applicant delivers to the division a certified copy of the final judgment of a court of competent jurisdiction establishing the applicant's right to use the name in this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(4): A name is distinguishable from other names, trademarks, and service marks registered with the division if the name contains one or more different words, letters, or numerals from other names upon the division's records.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5): The following differences are not distinguishing:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(a): the term:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(a)(i): decentralized autonomous organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(a)(ii): DAO;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(a)(iii): limited liability decentralized autonomous organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(a)(iv): L.L.D. or L.L.DAO; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(a)(v): L.D. or L.DAO;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(b): an abbreviation of a word listed in Subsection (5)(a);
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(c): the presence or absence of the words or symbols of the words "the," "and," "a," or "plus";
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(d): differences in punctuation and special characters;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(e): differences in capitalization; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(5)(f): differences in singular and plural forms of words.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(6): The division may not approve for filing a name that implies that a decentralized autonomous organization is an agency of this state or any of the state's political subdivisions, if the decentralized autonomous organization is not actually such a legally established agency or subdivision.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(7): The authorization to reserve or register a decentralized autonomous organization name as granted by the division does not:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(7)(a): abrogate or limit the law governing unfair competition or unfair trade practices;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(7)(b): derogate from the common law, the principles of equity, or the statutes of this state or of the United States with respect to the right to acquire and protect names and trademarks; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(7)(c): create an exclusive right in geographic or generic terms contained within a name.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8): The name of a decentralized autonomous organization may not contain:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(a): the term:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(a)(i): association;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(a)(ii): corporation;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(a)(iii): incorporated;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(a)(iv): partnership;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(a)(v): limited liability company;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(a)(vi): limited partnership; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(a)(vii): L.P.;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(b): any word or abbreviation that is of like import to the terms listed in Subsection (8)(a);
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(c): without the written consent of the United States Olympic Committee, the words:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(c)(i): Olympic;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(c)(ii): Olympiad; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(c)(iii): Citius Altius Fortius; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(8)(d): the number sequence 911.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(9): A person, other than a decentralized autonomous organization formed under this chapter or another decentralized autonomous organization that is authorized to transact business in this state, may not use in the person's name in this state the term:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(9)(a): limited liability decentralized autonomous organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(9)(b): limited decentralized autonomous organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(9)(c): L.L.DAO or L.L.D; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-105(9)(d): L.DAO or L.D.

Each decentralized autonomous organization shall designate a registered agent in this state in accordance with Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-107(2): (1) for affixing the seal to a certified copy described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108 Certificates issued by the division.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(1): Any person may apply to the division for:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(1)(a): a certificate of existence for a decentralized autonomous organization; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(1)(b): a certificate that sets forth any facts of record in the division.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(2): A certificate of existence or certificate of authorization sets forth:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(2)(a): the decentralized autonomous organization's name;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(2)(b): that the decentralized autonomous organization is recognized under the law of this state;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(2)(c): the date of the decentralized autonomous organization's formation;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(2)(d): that articles of dissolution have not been filed by the division; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(2)(e): other facts of record in the division that may be requested by the applicant.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-108(3): Subject to any qualification stated in the certificate, a certificate issued by the division may be relied upon as conclusive evidence of the facts set forth in the certificate.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201 Formation requirements.
------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(1)(a): One or more persons may act as organizers to form a decentralized autonomous organization by delivering to the division for filing a certificate of organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(1)(b): At least one of the organizers of a decentralized autonomous organization shall be an individual.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(2): 48-5-105; 16-17-203
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(2)(a): 48-5-105; 16-17-203 A certificate of organization shall provide:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(2)(a)(i): 48-5-105 the name of the decentralized autonomous organization, which shall comply with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(2)(a)(ii): the name of an organizer that is an individual;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(2)(a)(iii): the street and mailing address of the organizer described in Subsection (2)(a)(ii);
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(2)(a)(iv): the name and address of the legal representative; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(2)(a)(v): 16-17-203 the information required by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(2)(b): An organizer may request that the information provided in Subsections (2)(a)(ii) and (iii) is redacted by the division before any public disclosure of the filing.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3): A decentralized autonomous organization shall submit evidence to the division in a form required by the division that the decentralized autonomous organization has complied with the following requirements:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(a): the decentralized autonomous organization is deployed on a permissionless blockchain;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(b): the decentralized autonomous organization has a unique public address through which an individual can review and monitor the decentralized autonomous organization's transactions;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(c): the software code of the decentralized autonomous organization is available in a public forum for any person to review;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(d): the software code of the decentralized autonomous organization has undergone quality assurance;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(e): the decentralized autonomous organization has a graphical user interface that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(e)(i): allows a person to read the value of the key variables of the decentralized autonomous organization's smart contracts;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(e)(ii): allows a person to monitor all transactions originating from, or addressed to, the decentralized autonomous organization's smart contracts;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(e)(iii): specifies the restrictions on a member's ability to redeem tokens;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(e)(iv): makes available the decentralized autonomous organization's by-laws; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(e)(v): displays the mechanism to contact the administrator of the decentralized autonomous organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(f): the governance system of the decentralized autonomous organization is decentralized;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(g): the decentralized autonomous organization has at least one member;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(h): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(h)(i): there is a publicly specified communication mechanism that allows a person to contact the registered agent of the decentralized autonomous organization and provide legally recognized service; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(h)(ii): a member or administrator of the decentralized autonomous organization is able to access the contents of this communication mechanism; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(i): the decentralized autonomous organization describes or provides a dispute resolution mechanism that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(i)(i): binding on the decentralized autonomous organization, the members, and participants of the decentralized autonomous organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(3)(i)(ii): able to resolve disputes with third parties capable of settlement by alternative dispute resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(4): Notwithstanding the requirements of Subsection (3)(e)(iv), a decentralized autonomous organization may redact sensitive information from the by-laws before making the by-laws available, if those redactions are necessary to protect the privacy of individual members or participants in the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(5): A decentralized autonomous organization is formed when the decentralized autonomous organization's certificate of organization becomes effective and the decentralized autonomous organization submits the evidence required in Subsection (3).
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-201(6): 48-5-202 Upon formation, the decentralized autonomous organization shall have limited liability, subject to the provisions of Section


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-202 Limited liability.
-------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-202(1): (2); (3) Except as set forth in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-202(1)(a): may only be liable for the on-chain contributions that the member has committed to the decentralized autonomous organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-202(1)(b): may not be held personally liable for any excess liability after the decentralized autonomous organization's assets have been exhausted;
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-202(1)(c): may not be held personally liable for any obligation incurred by the decentralized autonomous organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-202(1)(d): may not be held personally liable, in the member's capacity as a member, for the wrongful act or omission of any other member of the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-202(2): If a decentralized autonomous organization refuses to comply with an enforceable judgment, order, or award entered against the decentralized autonomous organization, the members who voted against compliance may be liable for any monetary payments ordered in the judgment, order, or award in proportion to the member's share of governance rights in the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-202(3): (1); (2) Subsections


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-203 By-laws.
---------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-203(1): A decentralized autonomous organization shall adopt by-laws that establish internal organization and procedures for the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-203(2): The by-laws shall be set out in plain terms.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-203(3): The by-laws of a decentralized autonomous organization may contain any provision for managing the entity and regulating the affairs of the decentralized autonomous organization that is not inconsistent with law.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-204 Annual report to the division.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-204(1): 16-17-203(1) A decentralized autonomous organization shall deliver to the division for filing an annual report that states:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-204(1)(a): the name of the decentralized autonomous organization; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-204(1)(b): 16-17-203(1) the information required by Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-204(2): Information in the annual report must be current as of the date the report is signed by the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-204(3): (1) Every 12 months after the decentralized autonomous organization has been issued a certificate of organization, the decentralized autonomous organization shall submit the annual report described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-301 Classes of participation rights -- Membership.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-301(1): A decentralized autonomous organization's by-laws may create multiple classes of member participation rights.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-301(2): Where the decentralized autonomous organization has tokens providing governance powers to the token holder, the token holder shall be considered a member of the decentralized autonomous organization:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-301(2)(a): from the time the ownership of the tokens is established to be in the possession of an address; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-301(2)(b): from the time when ownership is first acknowledged by the token holder through an on-chain interaction with the decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-301(3): This section does not apply in the event of a hard fork.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-302 Voting rights.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-302(1): The by-laws shall set out the distribution of voting rights for the classes of member participation rights in a decentralized autonomous organization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-302(2): The method by which these voting rights are computed and distributed shall be set out in the by-laws.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-303 Proxies.
---------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-303(1): A member may be represented by a proxy.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-303(2): The by-laws of a decentralized autonomous organization may establish the requirements for representation by proxy.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-303(3): A proxy may exercise all rights of a member.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-304 Minority rights protection.
----------------------------------------------------------
The decentralized autonomous organization shall state in the by-laws whether the decentralized autonomous organization provides minority rights protection.

Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-305 Administrators.
----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-305(1): Unless mandated in the decentralized autonomous organization's by-laws, a decentralized autonomous organization is not required to have an administrator, including a board of directors or a trustee.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-305(2): In the absence of a provision requiring administrators, all the powers and tasks of an administrator shall be vested in the decentralized autonomous organization members as a class.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-305(3): The voting mechanism for nominating and appointing an administrator shall be set out in the decentralized autonomous organization's by-laws.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-306 Legal representation.
----------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-306(1): A decentralized autonomous organization shall retain a legal representative to undertake tasks that cannot be achieved on-chain.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-306(2): Legal representation of the decentralized autonomous organization shall be carried out by the legal representative in the manner provided in the by-laws, as evidenced by an authorization displayed on a public forum, and verifiable by cryptographic proof.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-306(3): The legal representative may undertake and execute any and all acts and contracts included within the scope of such authorization.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-306(4): The legal representative may not be required to reside in Utah.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-306(5): A legal representative may not be personally liable for acts performed on behalf of the decentralized autonomous organization.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-307 No implicit fiduciary status.
------------------------------------------------------------
A developer, member, participant, or legal representative of a decentralized autonomous organization may not be imputed to have fiduciary duties towards each other or third parties solely on account of their role, unless the developer, member, participant, or legal representative:Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-307(1): explicitly holds themselves out as a fiduciary; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-307(2): stipulates to assume a fiduciary status as provided in the decentralized autonomous organization's by-laws.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-401 Asset subscription and payment.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-401(1): No minimum capital requirements may apply to a decentralized autonomous organization recognized by this act.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-401(2): If the decentralized autonomous organization wishes to maintain a minimum amount of capital, the by-laws of the decentralized autonomous organization shall specify the rules for subscription and payment.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-401(3): The by-laws shall provide the rules for exiting the decentralized autonomous organization that address the consequences of voluntary and involuntary member and participant exit on subscriptions and payments made by the member or participant.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-401(4): No member may compel the dissolution of the decentralized autonomous organization for failure to return the member's on-chain contribution.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-402 Meetings.
----------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-402(1): A decentralized autonomous organization may hold meetings as provided in the decentralized autonomous organization's by-laws.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-402(2): Unless explicitly specified in the by-laws, meetings are not required to be in person.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-402(3): If the by-laws include a meeting requirement, the by-laws shall include an explicit and transparent mechanism of giving notice of meetings to administrators, members, or participants, and a defined time period for deliberating upon proposals submitted by an administrator, member, or participant.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-402(4): Notice of any required meeting shall be communicated through a graphical user interface.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-402(5): The quorum and majority requirements for meetings of a decentralized autonomous organization's administrators, members, or participants shall be specified in the by-laws.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403 Contentious forks in the underlying blockchain.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403(1): Except as provided in this section, in the event of a hard fork in the underlying permissionless blockchain:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403(1)(a): the legal representation of the decentralized autonomous organization remains on the majority chain; and
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403(1)(b): any off-chain assets shall belong to the decentralized autonomous organization on the majority chain.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403(2)(a): A decentralized autonomous organization may choose to maintain legal presence on a minority chain if the decentralized autonomous organization expresses an intent to do so by public signal.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403(2)(b): If the decentralized autonomous organization expresses an intent by public signal to maintain legal presence on a minority chain, any off-chain assets shall belong to the decentralized autonomous organization on the selected minority chain.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403(3): The decentralized autonomous organization may liquidate the decentralized autonomous organization's on-chain assets after a hard fork to move those assets to the chosen chain.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-403(4): The decentralized autonomous organization may split into multiple legal entities after a hard fork, each on a separate chain, after public signal of an intent to do so, provided there is a definitive distribution of off-chain assets between the majority and minority chain.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-404 Restructuring.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-404(1): 48-5-201 When a decentralized autonomous organization is restructured, whether through modification, upgrade, or migration, the decentralized autonomous organization's legal personality and limited liability is retained only to the extent that:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-404(1)(a): 48-5-201 the new software code of the decentralized autonomous organization fulfills all the formation requirements of Section
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-404(1)(b): where the decentralized autonomous organization has to be associated with a new unique public address, proper notice is provided by way of public signal.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-404(2): (1) A decentralized autonomous organization that is restructured in compliance with Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-405 Failure event.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-405(1): In the case of a failure event, legal personality and limited liability are maintained to the extent necessary to protect decentralized autonomous organization members and participants from personal liability.
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-405(2): A failure event may trigger liability on the person deploying or upgrading the decentralized autonomous organization if that person:
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-405(2)(a): acted in bad faith; or
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-405(2)(b): engaged in gross negligence.


Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-406 Taxation.
----------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-406(1): Title 59, Chapter 7, Corporate Franchise and Income Taxes If a decentralized autonomous organization recognized by this act is eligible to elect to be classified as a corporation for federal tax purposes, and the decentralized autonomous organization makes that election, the decentralized autonomous organization shall be subject to the provisions of
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-406(2): (1); Title 59, Chapter 10, Part 14, Pass-Through Entities and Pass-Through Entity Taxpayers Act
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-406(2)(a): (1); Title 59, Chapter 10, Part 14, Pass-Through Entities and Pass-Through Entity Taxpayers Act Unless the decentralized autonomous organization makes the election described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 48-5-406(2)(b): For purposes of taxation, a decentralized autonomous organization shall allocate the distributive share of income, gain, loss, deduction, and credit derived from the decentralized autonomous organization's activities, to each member of the decentralized autonomous organization in proportion to the member's membership interest in the entity.
